### [1] [Enhancing Oracle Bone Inscription Recognition via Multi-Scale Layer Attention](https://arxiv.org/abs/2607.00057)
*Chaowen Yan,Kaishen Wang,Yong Wang,Jianlong Xiong,Tao He*

Main category: cs.CV

TL;DR: 提出用于甲骨文识别的多尺度层注意力（MSLA），在大规模数据集上优于现有注意力机制且高效。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 甲骨文字形复杂、退化严重、形变不规则，现有基于专家手工分析的方法耗时易错；通用深度学习与最新层级注意力虽提升细粒度依赖建模，但在OBIs上改进有限，亟需能同时捕获多尺度与跨层细节的机制。

Method: 设计MSLA：显式建模多尺度与跨层特征交互，将不同空间尺度的细粒度信息与层间依赖融合，以增强表示；在大规模甲骨文数据集上进行实验评估，并与多种注意力机制对比，同时关注计算效率。

Result: 在大规模OBIs数据集上，MSLA在识别精度上持续超越现有注意力方法，并保持计算开销可控/高效。

Conclusion: 多尺度+跨层的注意力建模能更充分捕获甲骨文的细节与变形，显著提升识别的准确性与鲁棒性，同时不显著增加计算成本，适合作为OBIs识别的新范式。

Abstract: Oracle Bone Inscriptions (OBIs) recognition plays a crucial role in understanding ancient Chinese culture. However, accurately recognizing OBIs remains highly challenging due to their complex, irregular, and often degraded shapes. Traditional methods rely on expert knowledge and manual analysis, which are time-consuming and error-prone. Although deep learning has greatly advanced general image recognition, existing methods struggle to capture the fine-grained details and subtle variations inherent in OBIs, resulting in limited performance. Even most recent and effective layer attention techniques are designed to capture fine-grained dependencies through enhanced inter-layer interactions, yet they still exhibit only marginal improvements in OBIs recognition. To address these limitations, we propose Multi-Scale Layer Attention (MSLA), a novel paradigm that explicitly models both multi-scale and cross-layer feature interactions. By enriching the representation with fine-grained details across multiple spatial scales, MSLA enables more accurate and robust OBIs recognition. Extensive experiments on large-scale OBIs datasets demonstrate that MSLA consistently outperforms existing attention mechanisms while maintaining computational efficiency.

</details>


### [2] [Joint Medical Image Enhancement and Segmentation with Diffusion-based Symbiotic Information Interaction](https://arxiv.org/abs/2607.00058)
*Ying Chen,Jinyue Li,Qiankun Li*

Main category: cs.CV

TL;DR: 提出DiSIINet：将图像增强与分割在扩散模型框架下深度耦合，通过SII跨注意力在反向扩散中双向交互，显著优于串联或独立方案。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 医学影像常受分辨率与质量限制，独立的增强预处理无法与分割形成协同，导致病灶与结构识别受损，需要一个能让增强与分割互相促进的一体化方法。

Method: 以DDIM为骨干，构建增强分支与分割分支，在反向扩散阶段引入SII（Symbiotic Information Interaction）模块，通过跨注意力在特征层面进行动态信息交换，实现两任务的迭代互促；利用DDIM确定性采样提升推理效率与输出稳定性。

Result: 在多模态医学数据（MRI、CT、超声）上，相比顺序式或相互独立的增强与分割方法，取得显著性能提升（摘要未给出具体数值）。

Conclusion: 将增强与分割在扩散框架内联合建模并通过SII进行特征级交互，可提升图像质量与分割精度，具备跨模态泛化与高效推理潜力；代码已开源。

Abstract: Image quality is critical for accurate medical diagnosis. However, MRI, CT, and ultrasound images are often of low resolution and quality due to cost constraints, complicating the visualization of key anatomical structures and lesions. While such limitations are common in practice, traditional methods treat image enhancement as a separate preprocessing step, failing to fully leverage its potential synergy with image segmentation. To address this, we propose DiSIINet (Diffusion-based Symbiotic Information Interaction Network), which is built on the principle that enhancement and segmentation should mutually reinforce each other in a unified model. Based on Denoising Diffusion Implicit Models (DDIM), DiSIINet integrates an enhancement branch and a segmentation branch. These branches interact through a novel Symbiotic Information Interaction (SII) module, which facilitates dynamic, feature-level information exchange via cross-attention during the reverse diffusion process. This design enables both tasks to iteratively improve each other. The DDIM backbone ensures high-quality output and efficient inference through deterministic sampling. Experiments on multi-modal medical datasets (MRI, CT, ultrasound) show that DiSIINet achieves significant performance improvements compared to sequential or independent enhancement and segmentation approaches. The code is available at: https://github.com/Reconsider80/DiSIINet.

</details>


### [3] [Synergistic Perception-Reasoning Governance: Grounding Medical MLLMs with Verifiable Anatomical Evidence](https://arxiv.org/abs/2607.00060)
*Rui Hao,Qiankun Li,Junyuan Mao,Linghao Meng,Dirui Xie,Dayu Tan,Zhigang Zeng*

Main category: cs.CV

TL;DR: 提出一种训练-free的双侧证据注入框架，通过ROI先验调制视觉激活与解剖坐标语义化锚定文本推理，减少MLLM在医疗VQA与报告生成中的幻觉，跨多模型多数据集显著提升准确性并降低幻觉率。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 临床VQA与放射学报告生成中的多模态大模型常在推理阶段产生与影像证据不一致的“幻觉”。现有缓解方法依赖再训练、外部知识库或繁琐后验校验，成本高、泛化差、流程复杂。需要一种无需再训练、可通用于不同模型与任务、同时兼顾感知与语言推理的简单有效方法。

Method: 提出“整体式、训练-free”的双侧证据注入：1) 视觉侧：用MedSAM得到ROI先验，对视觉编码器/跨模态层进行ROI引导的激活调制，重校准感知轨迹；2) 文本侧：将解剖学坐标映射为离散语义token，充当可验证的外部记忆，锚定语言推理；3) 任务感知动态路由器：依据任务语义在不同模态干预间自适应选择与权衡，兼顾感知落地与语言流畅。

Result: 在2类任务、5个数据集上，基于LLaVA-1.5-7B、LLaVA-Med-1.5-7B、Qwen3-VL-8B/32B、InternVL-3.5-8B/38B系统评测与可控消融/可视化显示：相较基线，封闭式准确率最高提升约6%，开放式幻觉率降低约35%，且跨模型与任务稳定有效。

Conclusion: 双侧证据注入无需再训练即可系统性缓解医疗多模态推理的幻觉问题，兼顾可泛化性与部署简便性；通过任务感知路由在感知与语言间取得平衡。代码开源，便于复现与扩展。

Abstract: Multimodal large language models (MLLMs) show strong promise for clinical VQA and radiology report generation, yet inference-time hallucinations still undermine trustworthy use: models can produce fluent conclusions that conflict with imaging evidence. Existing mitigation strategies typically rely on additional training, external retrieval/knowledge bases, or multi-stage post-hoc verification, which increases cost and pipeline complexity and often generalizes poorly across models and tasks.To address this, we propose a holistic, training-free evidence-injection framework that systematically mitigates hallucinations through dual-side evidence injection. By leveraging ROI priors acquired using MedSAM in our implementation, we recalibrate the visual perception trajectory via ROI-guided activation modulation while anchoring the textual reasoning trajectory by mapping anatomical coordinates into discrete semantic tokens as verifiable external memory. Then we introduce a task-aware dynamic router to select modality-specific interventions based on task semantics, balancing perceptual grounding and linguistic fluency. We conduct systematic evaluations on 2 tasks and 5 datasets using \texttt{LLaVA-1.5-7B}, \texttt{LLaVA-Med-1.5-7B}, \texttt{Qwen3-VL-8B/32B}, and \texttt{InternVL-3.5-8B/38B}. Controlled ablations and visualizations further validate the framework, which consistently outperforms baselines across medical benchmarks, improving close-ended accuracy by up to $\sim\mathbf{6}\%\uparrow$ and reducing open-ended hallucinations by $\sim\mathbf{35}\%\downarrow$. The code has been made available on GitHub: \href{https://github.com/Henry991115/SPRG}{\textcolor{blue}{https://github.com/Henry991115/SPRG}}.

</details>


### [4] [Lost in the Tail: Addressing Geographic Imbalance in Urban Visual Place Recognition](https://arxiv.org/abs/2607.00090)
*Zhiyao Shu,Jiacheng Yang,Yang Lu,Waishan Qiu,Chuan Li,Da Chen*

Main category: cs.CV

TL;DR: 提出DAPR，一个与模型无关的“分布感知”插件，用于解决城市场景VPR中的长尾分布：训练期重加权梯度、检索期按类紧致度做多尺度距离搜索；在SF‑XL上显著提升并在多基线与数据集上泛化。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 城市场景VPR数据呈严重长尾：热门地点图像多、冷门地点稀少，现有方法被丰富类别主导，导致模型偏向“常拍地点”，对稀疏区域定位失败，影响公平性与泛化。需要系统刻画并缓解这种不平衡。

Method: 提出Distribution-Aware Place Recognition（DAPR）框架：1）训练阶段的分布重平衡——在分类-检索管线中，对头/尾类的梯度贡献进行再加权（模型无关的插件式策略），缓解长尾偏置；2）检索阶段的分布感知——引入多尺度距离搜索，根据每一类的分布紧致度（per-class compactness）自适应地调整匹配与重排序，提升尾类召回。

Result: 在大规模SF‑XL基准上，相比先前的classification-retrieval基线，测试集v1提升18.3%，v2提升6.7%；并在SF‑XL、MSLS、Pitts30k的多种代表性VPR方法上带来一致增益，显示良好可迁移性与通用性。

Conclusion: 长尾分布是城市场景VPR的关键瓶颈。DAPR通过训练期梯度再平衡与检索期多尺度分布感知联合解决，显著提升定位性能，并作为即插即用模块在多方法多数据集上稳定泛化。

Abstract: Urban-scale Visual Place Recognition (VPR) aims to identify the geographic location of a query image by matching it against a geo-tagged database. While recent methods achieve impressive performance, they overlook a serious long-tailed problem hidden in urban-scale datasets, which biases the model towards locations with abundant images and ignores less-visited areas, causing models to systematically favor frequently photographed locations while failing in sparsely covered areas. In this paper, we systematically characterize this imbalance challenge and propose Distribution-Aware Place Recognition (DAPR), a model-agnostic plug-in framework that rebalances gradient contributions across head and tail classes. Additionally, within classification-retrieval pipelines, DAPR applies a multi-scale distance search mechanism to compute per-class distributional compactness, providing complementary gains at the retrieval stage. On the large-scale SF-XL benchmark, our framework outperforms the previous classification-retrieval baseline by 18.3% on test set v1, and 6.7% on test set v2. As a plug-in module, it achieves consistent improvements across representative VPR methods on SF-XL, MSLS, and Pitts30k, demonstrating broad generalizability across different methods and benchmarks.

</details>


### [5] [PixelEyes: Decoupling Perception and Reasoning for Pinpoint Visual Evidence Seeking](https://arxiv.org/abs/2607.00115)
*Dengxian Gong,Yuanzheng Wu,Haobo Yuan,Zhengdong Hu,Tao Zhang,Yikang Zhou,Shihao Chen,Quanzhu Niu,Kai Wang,Jason Li,Haochen Wang,Lu Qi,Shunping Ji,Ming-Hsuan Yang*

Main category: cs.CV

TL;DR: 提出PixelEyes，将推理与感知解耦：用分割掩码做精确定位、以语义区域的广度优先搜索避免无效回溯，并构建PixelEyes-6K与Pinpoint-Bench以评测并分析定位与推理失误。结果显示现有MLLM在新基准上仍有较大提升空间。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 多轮视觉推理中，通用MLLM常因定位不准而反复纠错，造成冗长、低效的推理轨迹。根因是将“想什么”(推理)与“看哪里”(感知定位)耦合在同一模型中，定位误差会诱发额外推理回合。作者希望通过显式解耦，缩短轨迹、提高定位与推理的可靠性。

Method: 提出PixelEyes代理，显式分工：Reasoner决定“找什么”；专门的感知工具回答“在哪”。关键组件：1) Mask-guided Visual Search：调用指代表达分割模型输出实例级掩码，实现像素精度定位，避免Reasoner为粗糙对齐背锅。2) Semantic-region BFS：以语义区域为节点进行广度优先探索，减少因反复裁错子图带来的回路与遗漏。为内化能力，重合成专家轨迹形成PixelEyes-6K数据集，将掩码搜索与BFS策略显式注入模型。另构建Pinpoint-Bench零提示视觉搜索基准，提供实例级掩码与框，区分定位失败与推理失败。

Result: 在Pinpoint-Bench上，近期SOTA的MLLM与多轮视觉代理均显著落后，显示该基准的难度与有效性。PixelEyes通过精确定位与有序探索，显著减少冗余轨迹并提升成功率（文中定性/定量表明优势）。

Conclusion: 将推理与感知解耦、以掩码级定位与语义BFS组织探索，可有效缓解多轮视觉推理中的定位-推理纠缠与冗余问题。新数据集与基准支持细粒度误差诊断，揭示现有方法在零提示搜索上的明显不足；代码与模型已开源。

Abstract: This paper explores multi-turn visual reasoning and observes that MLLMs repeatedly fail to localize the target, leading to long, redundant trajectories. We attribute this failure to the entanglement of reasoning and perception within a single model, the MLLM reasons and localizes simultaneously, and inaccurate localization triggers additional reasoning turns that bloat the trajectory. To solve this problem, we propose PixelEyes, a multi-turn visual reasoning agent that explicitly decouples reasoning from perception, i.e., the reasoner decides what to look for, while a specialized perception tool answers where it is. Specifically, PixelEyes introduces 1) Mask-guided Visual Search. A referring segmentation model is invoked to provide mask-precise localization, freeing the reasoner from the need to compensate for imprecise grounding. 2) Semantic-region Breadth-first Search (BFS). To eliminate redundant loops caused by repeatedly cropping incorrect sub-regions, we organize exploration as a breadth-first search over semantic regions. To internalize these capabilities, we construct the PixelEyes-6K dataset by resynthesizing expert trajectories from existing data. This explicitly embeds our mask-guided search and BFS logic into the model. We further introduce Pinpoint-Bench, a zero-hint visual search benchmark, i.e., no location cues are provided in the question, with instance-level masks and bounding boxes that separate localization failures from reasoning failures, enabling fine-grained analysis of failure modes such as inattentional blindness. Recent state-of-the-art MLLMs and visual reasoning agents leave large headroom on Pinpoint-Bench, demonstrating its quality and difficulty. Code and models are open-sourced.

</details>


### [6] [Segmenting, Fast and Slow: Real-Time Open-Vocabulary Video Instance Segmentation with Dual-Path Processing](https://arxiv.org/abs/2607.00124)
*Luca Barsellotti,Martin Sundermeyer,Mattia Segu,Nikita Araslanov,Muhammad Ferjad Naeem,Marcella Cornia,Yongqin Xian,Maxim Berman*

Main category: cs.CV

TL;DR: 提出SegFS：一种双支路快-慢框架，将开放词汇视频实例分割中的实例传播从对象解码转为特征空间调制，在保持精度下大幅提升移动端实时性。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现有受DETR启发的对象中心OV-VIS方法虽在像素解码、文本融合和对象解码上做了轻量化，但高帧率、端侧实时推理仍困难，延迟与计算开销过高。

Method: 采用“慢支路+快支路”的双流设计：在稀疏关键帧用开放词汇对象模型预测实例级表示；将这些表示投影回骨干特征空间，用作条件信号驱动一个轻量快网络，在随后的非关键帧中快速再定位并分割目标。通过把实例传播从对象解码阶段转移到特征空间条件化，实现语义理解（多模态）与密集掩码预测的解耦与高效时域传播。

Result: 在标准OV-VIS基准上保持具有竞争力的分割精度，同时相较移动端取向的MOBIUS快支路可达最高14倍的时延降低。

Conclusion: SegFS在不显著牺牲准确性的前提下显著提升端侧OV-VIS推理效率，证明了通过特征空间条件化进行实例时序传播的有效性与可扩展性。

Abstract: Object-centric models inspired by DETR have become the dominant paradigm for open-vocabulary video instance segmentation (OV-VIS). While recent efforts have reduced the computational cost of pixel decoding, textual modality fusion, and object decoding to make these architectures more suitable for mobile devices, real-time on-device inference at high frame rates remains an open challenge. In this paper, we introduce SegFS, a dual-stream fast-slow framework that significantly improves efficiency without sacrificing accuracy. On sparse keyframes, an open-vocabulary object-based model predicts instance-level representations. These representations are then projected back into the backbone feature space to condition a lightweight fast network, which efficiently relocalizes and segments the instances in subsequent frames. By shifting instance propagation from object decoding to feature-space conditioning, our approach decouples multimodal semantic understanding from dense mask prediction and enables efficient temporal propagation. The proposed fast branch achieves up to 14x lower latency than the mobile-oriented MOBIUS model, while maintaining competitive segmentation performance on standard OV-VIS benchmarks.

</details>


### [7] [Decompose, Compare, and Decide: Multimodal LLMs are Implicit Few-Shot Learners](https://arxiv.org/abs/2607.00125)
*Yunhan Wang,Eshika Khandelwal,Edson Araujo,Walid Bousselham,Nina Shvetsova,Hilde Kuehne*

Main category: cs.CV

TL;DR: 提出DeCoDe：将少样本分类分解为成对图像二分类，用MLLM无需训练即可做强few-shot分类；用“是否同类”的肯定logit作相似度，并结合高层域信息，在12个多域基准上显著超越SOTA。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: MLLM在图像理解上很强，但直接用于少样本分类效果不稳定。需要一种无需再训练、可泛化到不同领域的数据稀缺场景的方法，充分利用MLLM已具备的视觉-语言能力。

Method: 把N类K-shot分类转化为多次二元对比：对查询图像与每个候选类的支持图像逐一比较，通过提示让MLLM回答“两图是否同类”。取“是”的logit作为相似度，汇总后将查询分配给最高分的类；并加入高层先验（如数据域/类别粒度等）提升判别。对不同推理变体进行系统评估。

Result: 在12个数据集（6个既有、6个新建、跨多种域）上，简单分解策略将现成MLLM变成强few-shot学习者，显著优于当前SOTA，包括标准与新颖领域；消融显示提供域级信息可进一步提升性能。

Conclusion: 将few-shot分类重构为成对一致性判断，利用MLLM的对比能力和高层先验，可在零/少训练下取得强性能，是一种通用、易用、可扩展的few-shot分类方案。

Abstract: Multimodal Large Language Models (MLLMs) have demonstrated remarkable abilities when analyzing images, yet translating these capabilities to few-shot image classification remains challenging. To bridge this gap, we present DeCoDe, a simple yet effective technique that enables off-the-shelf MLLMs to act as strong few-shot classifiers without any additional training. Our approach builds on the idea of few-shot classification as a set of pairwise image comparisons, decomposing the task into a set of binary decisions. Given a query image and a support image from a candidate class, the MLLM is prompted to decide whether the two images depict the same class. The logit corresponding to an affirmative response is then used as a similarity score to assign the query image to the most likely class. While this already yields good results, we show that providing additional high-level information, such as the data domain, to the model further improves performance. Our evaluation provides an extensive analysis of various inference variants on a suite of twelve datasets, six established and six newly curated few-shot benchmarks spanning across diverse domains. The results show that the proposed simple decomposition technique can turn off-the-shelf MLLMs into powerful few-shot learners, significantly outperforming current state-of-the-art few-shot methods on both standard and novel domains. Code is available at https://github.com/yunhanwang1105/DeCoDe.

</details>


### [8] [A Synthetic-Driven Vision System for Assembly Step Recognition](https://arxiv.org/abs/2607.00129)
*Hui Zhang,Xuanang Lei,Rui Wang,Julian Ferchow,Mirko Meboldt*

Main category: cs.CV

TL;DR: 提出一套基于合成数据的装配过程实时质检系统：用CAD与步骤描述在1小时内自动生成真实感装配序列，通过物理运动生成+域随机渲染+基于检测的步骤识别，实现强鲁棒的sim-to-real转移，在真实装配上达92.4%准确率。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 工业装配质检需要实时监控以避免代价高昂的缺陷，但收集标注任务特定的真实数据成本高、耗时长，限制了视觉质检模型的部署效率与泛化性。

Method: 构建端到端合成到实用的训练管线：1) 物理驱动的运动生成模块模拟多样化的人为装配轨迹与时序；2) 域随机渲染覆盖环境光照、材质与背景变化，提升对复杂工况的鲁棒性；3) 以目标检测为核心的步骤识别模型，利用零/少真实数据进行训练并实现稳健的sim-to-real迁移。系统仅需CAD模型与简单步骤文本，即可在约1小时内为特定任务生成数据并训练模型。

Result: 在真实工业装配案例上达到92.4%步骤识别准确率。相较无相应模块的基线，物理运动生成、域随机渲染、检测式识别分别带来46.7%、15.8%和61.2%的性能提升。

Conclusion: 合成数据驱动的装配质检方案在不依赖昂贵真实数据的前提下实现高精度与快速落地，验证了基于物理的多样化生成、域随机化与检测式识别对sim-to-real的关键作用，具有实际工业部署价值。

Abstract: Quality control in industrial assembly is essential, and real-time monitoring of the assembly process is crucial for preventing costly defects and ensuring production reliability. Vision-based automated inspection offers a powerful solution for such real-time monitoring. However, due to the specialized industrial components and processes, training these models typically relies on task-specific real-world data, which is costly and labor-intensive to collect and annotate. In this paper, we propose a system that automatically generates realistic assembly sequences and further trains real-time inspection models using the synthetic data. It can be efficiently applied to a given task within an hour, requiring only CAD models and simple step descriptions. Focusing on practical challenges, our system integrates a physics-based motion generation module to capture the variance of different human assembly, designs domain-randomized rendering to deal with the environmental complexity and variation, and employs an object-detection-based step recognition module for robust sim-to-real transfer, leading to 92.4% accuracy on a real-world assembly case with 46.7%, 15.8% and 61.2% performance improvement, respectively. Overall, our system provides a practical solution for industrial assembly inspection without requiring expensive real-world data collection and annotation, with the effectiveness validated on real industrial assembly tasks.

</details>


### [9] [MG-SpaIR: Multi-grade Sparse-guided Implicit Representation for Training-Data-Free Image Restoration](https://arxiv.org/abs/2607.00138)
*Jianmin Liao,Lei Huang,Ronglong Fang,Ashley Prater-Bennette,Lixin Shen,Yuesheng Xu*

Main category: cs.CV

TL;DR: MG-SpaIR 是一种无需训练数据的单幅图像混合退化恢复方法，基于隐式神经表示并采用多级粗到细残差层次与稀疏近端正则化，通过多级近端交替优化在理论保证下稳定收敛，实验优于 DIP 等强基线。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现有无需训练数据的单图像恢复（如 DIP/INR）常受频谱偏置与伪高频伪影影响，且对混合退化（模糊、降采样、噪声、缺失像素）难以稳定高保真重建。作者希望在不依赖外部数据的前提下，提升表示能力、抑制伪影并获得可收敛的优化流程。

Method: 以隐式神经表示为骨架，提出多级（multi-grade）粗到细的残差层次结构：逐级在更高分辨率上细化重建，缓解 INR 的频谱限制并提升表达精度；在高分辨率图像域显式施加稀疏近端正则（如ℓ0型），抑制伪高频同时保留锐利结构；采用多级近端交替优化方案高效求解，并给出在标准正则性条件下的收敛性保证。

Result: 在混合退化基准上，MG-SpaIR 在 PSNR/SSIM 等指标上稳定优于无需训练数据的强基线（如 Deep Image Prior），重建更清晰、伪影更少、优化更稳定。

Conclusion: MG-SpaIR 提供了一种稳定、可解释、数据高效的单图像混合退化恢复方案：通过多级 INR 残差与显式稀疏近端正则相结合，并配以有保证的近端交替优化，较现有无数据方法取得一致优势，可作为传统学习式恢复的替代。

Abstract: MG-SpaIR is a training-data-free framework for restoring a clean image from a single observation corrupted by a mixture of blur, downsampling, noise, and missing pixels. Building on implicit neural representations (INRs), we introduce a multi-grade coarse-to-fine residual hierarchy that progressively refines the reconstruction across resolution grades, improving representational fidelity and mitigating spectral limitations. To stabilize reconstruction optimization and suppress INR-induced artifacts, we further propose an explicit sparse proximal regularization (e.g., $\ell_0$-type) applied directly in the high-resolution image domain, which discourages spurious high-frequency patterns while preserving sharp structures. The resulting optimization is solved efficiently via a multi-grade proximal alternating scheme, and we establish convergence guarantees for the associated updates under standard regularity conditions. Experiments on mixed-degradation benchmarks demonstrate that MG-SpaIR consistently outperforms strong training-data-free baselines such as Deep Image Prior, providing a stable, interpretable, and data-efficient alternative to conventional learning-based restoration methods.

### [10] [A Mechanism-Driven Theory of Phase Transitions in Active Learning](https://arxiv.org/abs/2607.00144)
*Julia Machnio,Mads Nielsen,Mostafa Mehdipour Ghazi*

Main category: cs.CV

TL;DR: 论文将主动学习(AL)的“预算阶段”从固定标注数的经验划分，转化为由主导泛化机制更替所驱动的动态阶段划分，并以可观测代理与分段回归识别出数据驱动—过渡—模型驱动三阶段。不同采样策略在各阶段各擅胜场，且自监督表征可使阶段转折更早到来，从而提升样本效率。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现有AL常用“标注数量阈值”来区分早/中/后期，但该划分依赖数据集与模型，缺乏可迁移性，难以解释为何代表性、覆盖度、或不确定性策略在不同阶段表现迥异。需要一个能跨数据与架构泛化、并能解释性能随预算变化而非单点最优的统一动态框架。

Method: 理论上，将PAC风格的风险分解项重释为随预算变化彼此作用的动态项，证明主导项会随预算不可避免地发生转移，形成“移动瓶颈”。实践上，引入可测量代理指标并用分段回归自动检测阶段拐点，进而将AL过程划分为数据驱动、过渡、模型驱动三阶段，并分析各阶段与策略归纳偏置的匹配关系。

Result: 跨自然图像与医学影像实验证明：AL效率取决于策略的归纳偏置与当前主导瓶颈的对齐程度；代表性/覆盖/不确定性策略在不同阶段达到最佳；自监督学习改善表征使得“表征转移”更早发生，从而在相同标注预算下获得更高效率。

Conclusion: 将预算阶段视为主导泛化机制的动态更替，提供了统一、可观测、可检测的AL阶段划分框架，为设计“对转折敏感”的新一代AL算法提供指导：根据检测到的瓶颈动态切换或混合策略，尤其结合自监督以提前进入更高效阶段。

Abstract: Active learning (AL) performance is known to be budget-dependent, yet regimes are typically defined by heuristic label counts that fail to generalize across datasets or architectures. We characterize AL dynamics by reframing budget regimes as shifts in the dominant generalization mechanism. By reinterpreting PAC-style risk components as dynamic interacting terms, we prove that dominance shifts are structurally unavoidable, creating a moving bottleneck for generalization. We operationalize this using measurable proxies and a segmented regression procedure to identify a tripartite taxonomy: data-driven, transition, and model-driven phases. Our framework explains the long-standing observation that representativeness, coverage, and uncertainty strategies excel at different stages. Experiments across natural and medical imaging show that AL efficiency depends on the alignment between the strategy's inductive bias and the active bottleneck. Moreover, self-supervised representation shift transitions earlier along the labeling trajectory, highlighting the role of representation quality in shaping AL dynamics. Overall, this work provides a unified framework for the next generation of transition-aware AL algorithms.

*Siyuan Li,Weiying Chen,Yilin Wang,Xinxin Zuo,Xingyu Li,Li Cheng*

<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>

Method: 以粗形状先验为起点，结合3D Gaussian Splatting的测试时优化；采用对称感知的时间编码以利用双侧线索并吸收相机估计漂移；设计由可学习部件锚点与可学习蒙皮场引导的部件条件形变机制，实现姿态（关节运动）与非刚性形变的渐进解耦与优化。

Result: 在多物种数据上显著优于现有基线，表现为更高的几何精度、时间一致性与视觉保真度；即使先验与真实形状严重不匹配，仍具稳健泛化能力。

Abstract: Reconstructing 4D animals from monocular videos is challenging due to large inter-species variation, complex articulations, and the lack of reliable templates. Existing approaches typically rely on either strict category-specific priors that restrict generalization, or unconstrained generative models that sacrifice input fidelity. To bridge this gap, we present a progressive test-time optimization framework built on 3D Gaussian Splatting for high-fidelity 4D animal reconstruction from a single video. Our key insight is that a coarse shape prior suffices when coupled with a progressive strategy that disentangles articulated pose from non-rigid deformation. Specifically, we employ a symmetry-aware temporal encoding that exploits bilateral cues while absorbing camera estimation drift and a part-conditioned deformation mechanism guided by learnable part anchors and a learnable skinning field. Extensive experiments demonstrate that our approach generalizes robustly across diverse species, achieving superior geometric accuracy, temporal consistency, and visual fidelity compared to existing baselines, even under severe prior mismatch.

### [12] [Steal the Patch Size: Adversarially Manipulate Vision-Language Models](https://arxiv.org/abs/2607.00174)
*Kai Hu,Akash Bharadwaj,Weichen Yu,Matt Fredrikson*

Main category: cs.CV

TL;DR: 提出一种黑盒模型窃取方法，可从VLM推理接口中恢复其视觉分词器配置（如ViT补丁大小与预处理流程），通过在合成网格图上诱发周期性精度塌陷来估计补丁大小，并借助填充与一致性测试判定预处理分辨率与策略；在多种开源与专有模型上均有效，并可用于更强的迁移与定向对抗攻击。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: VLM的视觉分词器细节（补丁大小、缩放/填充策略、目标分辨率）通常未公开，但这些细节显著影响输入如何被离散化与感知，并决定了对抗样本与迁移攻击的有效性。作者希望在仅能黑盒访问模型的现实部署场景下，恢复这些“私有”配置，用于安全评估与揭示潜在的信息泄露风险。

Method: 利用ViT式patchification引入的任务级侧信道：构造可控周期的合成网格图，使网格线与隐含patch网格对齐时，边界在分词阶段被抹去，导致模型在某些周期处性能骤降。通过扫描网格单元尺寸，检测周期性准确率塌陷以反推出patch大小；再引入图像padding与一致性检查，区分动态/固定分辨率预处理并恢复目标缩放分辨率。

Result: 在开源的Qwen-VL系列与专有的GPT、Claude等VLM上，方法稳定恢复出视觉分词相关参数（补丁大小、是否固定/动态分辨率、目标resize大小）。

Conclusion: VLM的视觉分词与预处理参数会通过输入依赖的侧信道在黑盒设置下泄露；掌握这些参数能提升预处理感知的迁移攻击与针对模型定制的对抗操控效果，提示需要在系统层面与分词/预处理设计上采取缓解措施。

Abstract: We present a black-box model-stealing attack that recovers private vision-tokenizer configurations of deployed vision-language models (VLMs), including the visual patch size and input preprocessing pipeline. The key idea is a task-level side channel induced by ViT-style patchification: when a synthetic grid image is aligned with the hidden patch grid, boundary cues are erased at tokenization, causing periodic accuracy drop. By sweeping the grid cell size and measuring these collapses, we infer the patch size; by introducing padding and a consistency-check test, we further identify whether preprocessing is dynamic- or fixed-resolution and recover the target resize resolution. Across open-source Qwen-VL variants and proprietary models including GPT and Claude, we reliably recover tokenizer-related parameters. Finally, we show that such leakage enables preprocessing-aware transfer attacks and model-targeted adversarial manipulation.

### [13] [PRISM-VO: Scale-Aware Visual Odometry Using Photometric Plenoptic Bundle Adjustment](https://arxiv.org/abs/2607.00176)
*Aymeric Fleith,Julian Zirbel,Daniel Cremers,Niclas Zeller*

Main category: cs.CV

TL;DR: 提出PRISM-VO：一种面向焦平面全光相机（focused plenoptic）的纯优化稀疏光度视觉里程计，通过新型光度全光束调整在滑动窗口内联合优化位姿与点的逆深度，融合单幅全光几何深度与时序多视约束，实现高精度、低漂移、具度量尺度的运动估计，且无需复杂初始化，仅用单个全光传感器。实验在室内外优于现SOTA并可靠恢复尺度。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 传统单目SLAM存在尺度歧义和易漂移问题；全光相机可直接提供几何深度线索，但如何在VO中有效利用、并在仅用单传感器情况下获得鲁棒、度量尺度的估计仍是难题。需要一种能显式建模全光投影、联合利用光度与几何信息、又避免复杂初始化的VO方法。

Method: 构建光度全光束调整（plenoptic photometric BA），在滑动窗口内联合优化相机位姿和稀疏特征的逆深度；显式建模焦平面全光相机的投影与成像几何，从单帧全光图计算深度先验；将这些先验与时序多视光度误差结合，形成纯优化稀疏框架，无需学习；使用度量尺度的全光几何以消除尺度歧义。

Result: 在室内外数据上，PRISM-VO优于当前最先进的全光VO方法；与优化/学习方法相比，精度与稳健性具有竞争力，且能稳定恢复场景的度量尺度。

Conclusion: 通过把单帧全光深度与时序光度、多视约束在同一优化框架中联合建模，PRISM-VO实现了仅用单个全光传感器的高精度、低漂移、具度量尺度VO，避免复杂初始化并在多场景表现领先。

Abstract: We introduce PRISM-VO, a novel pure optimization-based sparse photometric visual odometry framework for focused plenoptic cameras. The core of PRISM-VO is a novel photometric plenoptic bundle adjustment which jointly optimizes camera poses and inverse depth values of points in a sliding window. By combining geometric depth from a single plenoptic image with temporal multi-view constraints, PRISM-VO achieves accurate and drift-resilient motion estimation. Through explicit modeling of the plenoptic projection, PRISM-VO provides reliable metric-scale reconstructions, overcoming the scale ambiguity of monocular SLAM algorithms. Importantly, our approach relies solely on a single plenoptic sensor and avoids complex initialization, as depth priors are computed directly from plenoptic imaging.
  Experiments show that PRISM-VO outperforms the current state-of-the-art plenoptic visual odometry method on indoor and outdoor scenes. The proposed approach rivals other optimization- and learning-based methods while accurately and reliably recovering a metric scale of the scene.
  Project page: https://prism-vo.github.io/

### [14] [DriftScope: Measuring The Hidden Effects of Diffusion Model Adaptation](https://arxiv.org/abs/2607.00183)
*Héctor Laria,Yiping Han,Julian D. Santamaria,Kai Wang,Bogdan Raducanu,Joost van de Weijer,Alexandra Gomez-Villa*

Main category: cs.CV

TL;DR: 论文指出：对文本到图像扩散模型进行适配（定制新概念或遗忘不良概念）会在无关概念上造成系统性“隐性漂移”，常用的整体指标（FID/KID）难以及时暴露；为此提出无需真实数据与内部访问的提示级诊断工具DriftScope，可排序给出在两次检查点之间漂移最大的词元。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现有评测只关注适配的目标效果，忽视对无关概念的副作用；而且聚合指标如FID/KID只有在模型几近失效时才显著变化，无法提前预警。需要一种能在概念层面定位和解释漂移的审计方法，以提升部署前的可靠性。

Method: 1) 通过稀疏自编码器与零样本分类对比，量化不同适配方式在无关概念上的损伤；2) 提出DriftScope：给定两个模型检查点，优化软提示以度量并归因于词元层面的视觉概念漂移，输出按漂移强度排序的Token列表；无需访问真实数据或模型内部权重细节。

Result: 发现无论是概念定制还是概念遗忘，权重级改动都会系统性伤及无关概念：当FID/KID有反应时模型已接近不可用；在模型仍可用时，FID/KID基本不变，但特定类别的零样本准确率最差可下降18.9个百分点，概念级分布发生显著偏移。DriftScope能够在部署前揭示这些隐性漂移，并给出可解释的Token级审计结果。

Conclusion: 适配扩散模型的副作用是普遍且结构性的，传统聚合指标难以及时发现。DriftScope提供了一种数据无关、可解释的概念级审计途径，可用于在部署前识别并定位漂移，从而更稳健地进行模型定制或遗忘。

Abstract: Adapting pre-trained text-to-image diffusion models, whether to learn new visual concepts or erase unwanted ones, is routinely evaluated on its intended effects alone. We argue this framing is incomplete. Through sparse autoencoder analysis and zero-shot classification, we demonstrate that adaptation systematically damages semantically unrelated concepts in ways that aggregate metrics structurally cannot surface: when damage is severe enough for FID and KID to respond, the model is already nearly unusable; when the model remains functional, FID and KID stay flat while specific classes silently suffer worst-case zero-shot accuracy drops of up to 18.9 points and concept-level distributions shift dramatically. This pattern appears at both ends of the adaptation spectrum (concept customization and concept unlearning), suggesting it is a systematic consequence of weight-level modification rather than an artifact of any particular method. To surface this hidden drift before deployment, we introduce DriftScope, a prompt-level diagnostic tool that takes any two model checkpoints and returns a ranked list of tokens whose visual concepts have shifted most between them. DriftScope optimizes a soft prompt to attribute drift at the token level without requiring access to real data or model internals. The result is an interpretable, concept-level audit that aggregate evaluation cannot provide.

</details>


### [15] [VOCA: Visual Odometry with Codec Awareness](https://arxiv.org/abs/2607.00189)
*Nouri Alexander Hilscher,Mateo de Mayo,Dominik Muhle,Christoph Otten genannt Hermes,Daniel Cremers*

Conclusion: 广泛可得的视频编码信息是视觉任务的宝贵信号；将其融入VO可显著提升压缩场景下的跟踪精度与效率，值得在更广泛的视觉系统中推广。

Abstract: Camera pose estimation from image streams is a critical component of spatial world models that integrate perception into planning and decision-making. Nearly all Visual Odometry (VO) and Simultaneous Localization and Mapping (V-SLAM) systems have focused on datasets containing raw, uncompressed videos. Many working systems instead use ubiquitous hardware units to efficiently compress and decode video streams, saving orders of magnitude in storage and bandwidth. However, this lossy compression introduces visual artifacts that hinder the performance of traditional tracking systems. We present VOCA, a causal stereo visual-odometry method that exploits codec information to improve tracking performance. We achieve state-of-the-art performance on causal VO for relative trajectory error, efficiency, and absolute trajectory error on compressed streams. This work highlights the potential of leveraging widely available video codec information for vision tasks.

### [16] [Trust the Prior (or Not): Uncertainty-Aware Abdominal Aortic Aneurysm Segmentation](https://arxiv.org/abs/2607.00201)
*Erich Robbi,Daniele Ravanelli,Andrea Passerini*

Main category: cs.CV

TL;DR: 提出一种患者特异性的AAA血管腔内血栓分割框架，通过解剖先验与不确定性引导注意力，配合基于局部解剖的GMM强度归一化，提升在分布内与多中心外部分布下的稳健性与可解释性，达成SOTA与更强泛化。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: AAA风险评估依赖血栓（ILT）精确分割，但ILT与周围非增强组织对比度低、形态/纹理异质，且不同CTA协议引发域偏移，导致多中心泛化差与临床可靠性不足。需要一种既利用解剖先验又能适应患者个体差异、并对不确定性具有鲁棒性的方案。

Method: 患者特异性两部分：1) 基于局部解剖的高斯混合模型（GMM）进行强度归一化，使不同CTA协议下的强度分布对齐；2) 不确定性门控的解剖注意力（UGAA），在分割网络中融合空间解剖先验，并按体素级置信度自适应调制先验贡献：在模糊区域加强先验，在低置信/不可靠先验处抑制。框架实现视觉证据与解剖证据的显式解耦，提升可解释性。

Result: 在同分布测试集上达到SOTA；在外部多中心CTA数据上显著优于现有方法，表现出更强的跨域泛化与稳健性。模型还能通过分离的视觉/解剖证据与不确定性图提供可解释输出。

Conclusion: 患者特异性的强度归一化与不确定性门控解剖注意力有效缓解低对比与域偏移问题，兼顾准确性、泛化与可解释性，适合临床多中心应用。

Domain shifts induced by different Computed Tomography Angiography (CTA) protocols further inhibit multi-center generalization of deep learning models. To address these challenges, we propose a patient-specific framework that integrates discriminative learning with anatomically informed priors. Our approach introduces two key components: (1) a patient-specific intensity normalization based on a Gaussian Mixture Model of local anatomy, and (2) an Uncertainty-Gated Anatomical Attention module that incorporates spatial priors while adaptively modulating their influence according to voxel-wise confidence. This design allows for anatomical guidance in ambiguous regions while suppressing unreliable priors. The proposed method achieves state-of-the-art performance on in-distribution test data and substantially outperforms existing alternatives in generalization to external multi-center CTA data, while remaining interpretable through an explicit separation of visual and anatomical evidence.

</details>


### [17] [EgoSafetyBench: A Diagnostic Egocentric Video Benchmark for Evaluating Embodied VLMs as Runtime Safety Guards](https://arxiv.org/abs/2607.00218)
*Siddhant Panpatil,Arth Singh,Mijin Koo,Chaeyun Kim,Haon Park,Dasol Choi*

Main category: cs.CV

TL;DR: 提出EgoSafetyBench评测VLM作为流式安全守卫：1,200段第一视角机器人视频，半秒标注，两大赛道与对照梯度。结果：VLM能识别含危险的视频但易错过具体时刻；情境性危险尤难。场内误导性文字显著削弱守卫：脆弱模型漏检多，稳健模型过度干预；表面稳健多为“狼来了”而非真实物理推理。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现实部署中，作为安保的VLM需精准区分真正不安全与“看似危险但实际常规”的场景；现有二元基准掩盖了这种细粒度差异。需要一个能在视频流中、依赖关键线索做出时序判断并检验对误导性文本抗扰性的基准。

Method: 构建EgoSafetyBench：1,200个自机器人视角的视频片段，0.5秒粒度标注；两条赛道。1) 情境赛道(800)：覆盖常规、安全但可疑、明显危险、情境性危险四类；用“对照梯子”——仅在单一可见决定性线索上差异的近似样本，迫使模型基于关键线索判断。2) 视觉文字赛道(400)：场景中可见标识/标签/贴纸成对出现（误导版vs真实版），评估模型能否识别文字误导并是否影响其物理安全判断。评测10个开源与闭源VLM，按流式守卫设定评估其对时刻与场景的判断。

Result: 总体能识别含危险的视频，但对具体危险发生的关键时刻召回不足，尤其在情境性危险上。场内误导性文字使所有模型性能下降：部分模型漏检高达约三分之一的危险；相对“稳健”的模型则对安全内容过度报警。配套对照显示，一些看似稳健性实为无差别高报警率，而非理解物理与情境。

Conclusion: 当前VLM作为运行时安全守卫仍不可靠：难以捕捉细粒度、情境依赖的危险时刻，且易被场内文字误导。需要改进对关键线索的时序敏感性与对文字-物理不一致的鲁棒推理，并用对照梯度式基准避免以高报警率伪装的“稳健性”。

Abstract: Vision-language models (VLMs) are now proposed as runtime safety guards for embodied agents in homes and factories. A deployable guard must catch genuinely unsafe situations while avoiding unnecessary intervention on routine but superficially alarming activity, a distinction that binary safety benchmarks obscure. We introduce EgoSafetyBench, an egocentric video benchmark of 1,200 robot-view scenarios annotated at half-second granularity, to evaluate VLMs as streaming guards across two tracks. The situational track (800 scenarios) spans four families, from routine and safe-but-suspicious scenes to obvious and contextual hazards. The visual-channel track (400 scenarios) targets in-scene text-a sign, sticker, or label visible in the scene-that can misrepresent the physical situation, pairing each misleading sign with a truthful version to test both whether a guard flags the text as misleading and whether the text corrupts its physical-safety judgment. Both tracks use contrastive ladders: near-identical scenarios differing only in a single visible deciding cue, so a correct call must hinge on that cue rather than the overall scene type. We evaluate ten open- and closed-source VLMs. We find that while guards reliably recognize videos containing hazards, they often miss specific hazardous moments, particularly contextual hazards. Furthermore, misleading in-scene signs degrade all tested guards: vulnerable models miss up to a third of hazards, while robust models over-intervene on safe content. Matched controls reveal that apparent safety robustness often reflects indiscriminate alarming rather than true physical reasoning.

### [18] [Does Your ViT Still Need U-Net for Segmentation?](https://arxiv.org/abs/2607.00223)
*Xin Li,Wenhui Zhu,Xuanzhao Dong,Xiwen Chen,Yanxi Chen,Yujian Xiong,Hao Wang,Oana M. Dumitrascu,Yalin Wang*

<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 传统医学分割多依赖U-Net解码器；早期ViT需解码器弥补表征不足。随着大规模预训练提升ViT能力，疑问在于：U-Net范式是否仍必需？若否，如何设计仅编码器框架以实现高精度密集预测。

Method: 使用现代ViT作为骨干，提出查询式encoder-only设计：多级查询建模（从不同层级特征中提取/更新查询表示）与可学习的block融合策略整合多层信息，无显式U-Net解码器。

Result: 在7个医学影像基准（CT、MRI、病理、内镜、皮肤镜）上验证，取得优异mDice：Synapse 85.50%、ACDC 91.73%、GlaS 93.27%，表现稳健且通用。

Abstract: Medical image segmentation is dominated by U-Net-style encoder-decoder architectures. Vision Transformers (ViTs) overcome the limited receptive field of convolutional networks through self-attention, enabling modeling of long-range dependencies. Early ViT-based segmentation methods typically retained U-Net-style decoders because pretrained ViT representations were insufficient to support accurate dense prediction. Recent advances in large-scale pretraining have redefined the representation capability of ViTs, reducing the reliance on U-Net-style decoder architectures in modern vision models. This prompts two questions: Is the U-Net paradigm still necessary for medical image segmentation? If not, how should an encoder-only segmentation framework be designed? Motivated by these questions, we explore key architectural choices for encoder-only medical image segmentation based on modern ViT backbones and establish a query-based encoder-only design with multi-level query modeling and learnable block fusion, realized in Encoder-only Segmentation (EoSeg). Extensive experiments across seven benchmark datasets spanning CT, MRI, histopathology, endoscopy, and dermoscopy validate the effectiveness of the proposed design across diverse medical imaging modalities, including mDice scores of 85.50% on Synapse, 91.73% on ACDC, and 93.27% on GlaS. The results demonstrate that a U-Net-style decoder is no longer necessary for medical image segmentation with modern ViT backbones and further show that EoSeg provides an effective encoder-only design. Code is available at: https://github.com/Retinal-Research/EoSeg

### [19] [Leveraging Phase Information to Boost Unrolled Network Learning for Image Deblurring](https://arxiv.org/abs/2607.00251)
*Samira Malek,Haichuan Zhang,Chul Lee,Vishal Monga*

Main category: cs.CV

TL;DR: 提出UPADNet：在频域进行幅度与相位分解并展开迭代优化，用LMMSE估计器先估幅度与相位，再以可学习矩阵参数端到端训练。相较现有解卷积与展开网络，在GoPro/RealBlur/COCO上更优，噪声高与小数据下优势更明显。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 传统去模糊多在空间域直接恢复像素，忽视了相位对锐利细节的关键作用；同时，固定的统计参数难以适应复杂退化与噪声。作者动机是显式建模并准确估计相位与幅度，并将统计估计与深度学习融合以提升鲁棒性与泛化。

Method: 1) 在频域对观测图像做幅度-相位分解；2) 推导模糊噪声观测下幅度与相位的LMMSE估计器；3) 设计迭代优化流程，用上述估计器交替更新并重建清晰图像；4) 将迭代算法展开为网络UPADNet，将其中的矩阵参数由数据驱动学习，端到端训练。

Result: 在GoPro、RealBlur、COCO基准上，UPADNet优于最先进深度网络（含空间域展开法）。在高噪声与训练样本受限时，性能提升更显著。

Conclusion: 相位—幅度显式分解结合LMMSE与可学习展开框架能更好恢复细节并具备鲁棒性。学习化的统计参数使方法在各种退化与噪声条件下均优于现有方法。

Abstract: While most image deblurring techniques directly restore the spatial image variable, we propose an amplitude and phase decomposition recognizing the importance of accurate phase estimation in recovering sharp image details. To that end, we first develop novel linear minimum mean squared (LMMSE) estimators of the amplitude and phase of the blurred, noisy image observation. An iterative optimization algorithm follows that recovers the sharp image using the aforementioned LMMSE estimators. Finally, matrix parameters that are statistically determined and fixed in the iterative algorithm are now learned using a training dataset of clean and degraded observations. Our deblurring engine is dubbed UPADNet (Unrolled Phase and Amplitude Decomposition Network), such that each iteration of the underlying phase and amplitude recovery algorithm is parameterized and trained end-to-end. Experiments over benchmark evaluation datasets such as GoPro, RealBlur and COCO datasets confirm that UPADNet outperforms state of the art deep networks including those based on algorithm unrolling in the image domain. The benefits of UPADNet are even more pronounced in high noise and limited training data regimes.

### [20] [Multi-Hypothesis Test-Time Adaptation to Mitigate Underspecification](https://arxiv.org/abs/2607.00259)
*Afshar Shamsi,Xiao-Yu Guo,Hamid Alinejad-Rokny,Arash Mohammadi,Damien Teney,Ehsan Abbasnejad*

Main category: cs.CV

TL;DR: 提出一种将测试时自适应（TTA）视为后验启发的多假设推断问题，通过粒子化多样化在输出、参数、优化器与输入四个层面并行探索多条低熵适配轨迹，以缓解熵最小化导致的欠设定与不稳定，作为即插即用外壳在多基线与多场景下带来稳定鲁棒增益。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 传统基于熵最小化的TTA在无监督条件下欠约束：许多参数更新都能达到类似低熵却对应截然不同的决策边界，易陷入伪模式并导致崩溃，缺乏稳定性与鲁棒性。亟需一种能系统探索多种合理解、降低欠设定风险的策略。

Method: 将熵最小化诱导的低熵解视为对参数的“伪似然”，不再求单点估计，而采用粒子化的多样化框架并行探索多条适配轨迹；在输出、参数、优化器、输入四个层面引入多样性，作为可插拔的包装器叠加在现有TTA方法之上。

Result: 在多种具有挑战的基准与分布移位设置下均提升稳定性与鲁棒性：混合移位提升约3-4%，batch size为1时提升约2-3%，标签移位提升约1-2.5%，整体优于最新SOTA基线。

Conclusion: 将TTA从单点优化转为多假设后验式推断，通过多层级粒子化多样化可以有效缓解欠设定，显著提高测试时适配的稳定性与可靠性，利于真实场景部署。

Abstract: Test-Time Adaptation (TTA) seeks to improve model robustness under distribution shifts by adapting parameters using unlabeled target data. However, in the absence of supervision, entropy-based adaptation is fundamentally underconstrained: multiple distinct parameter updates can achieve similarly low entropy while inducing drastically different decision boundaries. This phenomenon, known as underspecification, renders standard TTA brittle and prone to collapse into spurious modes. In this work, we reinterpret TTA through a posterior-inspired lens induced by entropy minimization, where low-entropy solutions define a pseudo-likelihood over parameters. Instead of committing to a single point estimate, we introduce a particle-based diversification framework that explores multiple plausible adaptation trajectories simultaneously. Our method can be viewed as a structured exploration of multiple plausible adaptation solutions, implemented through multi-level diversification at the output, parameter, optimizer, and input levels. Crucially, the framework acts as a plug-and-play wrapper compatible with existing TTA methods. Extensive experiments on challenging benchmarks demonstrate consistent gains in stability and robustness, achieving improvements of 3-4% under mixed shifts, 2-3% with batch size one, and 1-2.5% under label shifts, outperforming state-of-the-art baselines. Our results suggest that treating TTA as a multi-hypothesis inference problem, rather than a single-point optimization task, is key to mitigating underspecification and enabling reliable real-world deployment.

</details>


### [21] [MVDGC: Joint 3D and 2D Multi-view Pedestrian Detection via Dual Geometric Constraints](https://arxiv.org/abs/2607.00273)
*Thinh Phan,Hao Vo,Khoa Vo,Thanh Ngo,Cuong Pham,Ngan Le*

Main category: cs.CV

TL;DR: 提出MVDGC：用稀疏3D圆柱查询联合优化BEV行人定位与图像2D框，避免BEV投影失真并利用跨视角几何一致性，提升密集遮挡场景检测。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现有MVPD多将图像特征投影到BEV再定位，但透视变换导致失真与空间结构破坏，致使特征模糊、BEV点定位不准，尤其在人群密集处；同时2D检测与BEV定位间的强耦合关系未被联合利用，2D多视角一致性常仅作辅助信号。

Method: 引入统一框架MVDGC：以稀疏3D圆柱查询表示行人（柱心在BEV地面，投影为各视角矩形框），通过相机投影直接从原始图像特征采样，避免BEV投影失真；将BEV与图像视角定位转化为同一任务的3D圆柱位置与形状迭代细化，并以跨BEV与图像的双重几何约束实现联合优化。

Result: 在多视角行人检测场景中，实现更精确的BEV点定位与2D框预测，尤其在密集与遮挡严重区域取得显著提升（摘要未给出具体数值）。代码开源：github.com/UARK-AICV/MVDGC。

Conclusion: 通过3D圆柱查询作为几何形状锚，统一并耦合BEV与2D检测，避免投影失真并强化多视角一致性，从而提升MVPD的鲁棒性与精度。

Abstract: The core challenge in multi-view pedestrian detection (MVPD) lies in effective aggregation of visual features from different viewpoints for robust occlusion reasoning. Recent approaches have addressed this by first projecting image-view features onto a Bird's Eye View (BEV) map, where ground localization is then performed. Despite impressive performance, the perspective transformation induces severe distortion, causing spatial structure break and degrading the quality of object feature extraction. The blurred and ambiguous features hinder accurate BEV point localization, especially in densely populated regions. Moreover, the strong mutual relationship between the BEV ground point and image bounding boxes is not capitalized on. Although multi-view consistency of 2D detections can serve as a powerful constraint in BEV space, these detections are commonly treated as auxiliary signals rather than being jointly optimized with the primary task.In this work, we propose \textbf{MVDGC}, a unified framework that \emph{jointly estimates pedestrian locations on the BEV plane and 2D bounding boxes in image views}. MVDGC employs a \emph{sparse set of 3D cylindrical queries} that embraces geometric context across both BEV and image views, enforcing dual spatial constraints for precise localization. Specifically, the geometric constraints is established by modeling each pedestrian as a vertical cylinder whose center lies on the BEV plane and whose projection casts a rectangular box in the image views. These queries function as shape anchors that directly extract 2D features from the intact image-view features using camera projection, eliminating projection-induced distortions. The 3D cylindrical query enables the unification of BEV and ImV localization into a single task: 3D cylinder position and shape refinement. Code is available at: https://github.com/UARK-AICV/MVDGC

</details>

TL;DR: Aegis 是一个针对乳腺X线摄影同时进行癌症分诊与乳腺密度评估的联合嵌入预测架构（JEPA+ViT）。在大规模多机构数据自监督预训练、渐进分辨率微调后，取得高AUC，并在外部数据集实现零样本迁移。

Abstract: We present Aegis, a joint-embedding predictive architecture for breast cancer detection and density assessment in mammography. We train three Vision Transformer variants (Small/Base/Large) using self-supervised joint-embedding predictive architecture (JEPA) pre-training on 71,103 studies from 14 clinical sites, followed by supervised fine-tuning with progressive resolution scaling up to 2048x1536. On a curated 785-study test set, our largest model achieves area under the receiver operating characteristic curve (AUC) 0.949 for breast cancer triage with 93% sensitivity and 75% specificity at the optimal operating point. An ensemble combining our model with a U.S. Food and Drug Administration-cleared baseline further improves discrimination to 0.952 AUC. For breast density classification, the model achieves 0.953 AUC for binary (dense vs. non-dense) classification and 62.6% exact accuracy across four Breast Imaging Reporting and Data System (BI-RADS) categories, with 98.8% adjacent accuracy comparable to reported human inter-reader agreement. ### [23] [OnPoint: Offline-to-Online Multi-Level Distillation for Point-Supervised Online Temporal Action Localization](https://arxiv.org/abs/2607.00289)
*Sakib Reza,Gauri Jagatap,Mohsen Moghaddam,Octavia Camps,Andrea Fanelli*

<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>

Method: 构建离线教师与在线学生的“离线到在线”蒸馏：1) 伪段实例蒸馏：教师生成伪段监督学生的边界/实例级表示；2) 类激活序列蒸馏：对时间序列的类响应进行对齐；3) 预判窗口级蒸馏：面向未来的小窗口预测能力迁移。辅以：将原始点标直接纳入学生训练；以actionness引导的注意力校准来优化锚点解码与鲁棒性。

Conclusion: 点监督与多层次蒸馏可弥合离线与在线TAL差距；OnPoint为POTAL提供强基线与新范式，具备更高可扩展性与在线适用性。

Abstract: Temporal Action Localization (TAL) typically relies on segment annotations or offline access to full videos, limiting scalability and online use. We introduce Point-Supervised Online TAL (POTAL), which localizes actions in streaming videos using only one temporal point per instance. To solve POTAL, we propose OnPoint, an offline-to-online multi-level distillation framework that transfers knowledge from a point-supervised offline teacher to an online student via (i) pseudo-segment instance distillation, (ii) class-activation sequence distillation, and (iii) anticipatory window-level distillation. We further improve robustness by incorporating the original point labels into student training and by refining anchor decoding with actionness-guided attention calibration. Experiments on five datasets show OnPoint consistently outperforms strong baselines, establishing a solid foundation for POTAL.

### [24] [Rosetta: Composable Native Multimodal Pretraining](https://arxiv.org/abs/2607.00293)
*Xiangyue Liu,Zijian Zhang,Miles Yang,Zhao Zhong,Liefeng Bo,Ping Tan*

Main category: cs.CV

TL;DR: 提出Rosetta：一种可组合、原生多模态预训练框架，通过共享全局专家保持基础知识、插拔式专家承载模态特性，并用动量锚定正交投影（MAOP）化解新模态带来的梯度冲突，从而避免遗忘、实现无损扩展并提升图像生成与跨模态协同。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 多模态AGI需要不断接入新模态，但同时进行离散理解与连续生成训练时梯度冲突严重，主流MoE/MoT会出现表示被覆盖与灾难性遗忘，限制可扩展性。

Method: 1) 结构：全球共享专家存放通用基础知识；模态专属“可插拔”专家学习各自能力；以可组合方式扩展新模态。2) 训练：提出MAOP，用优化器动量作为语义锚，检测并正交投影/抑制与既有动量冲突的梯度分量，仅保留协同更新，从而保护旧知识。

Result: 在广泛评测中，标准MoE/MoT对已学语言与视觉能力出现明显遗忘；Rosetta在保持既有理解能力的同时，取得更好的图像生成质量，并展现跨模态协同增益。

Conclusion: Rosetta通过模块化专家与MAOP，实现对新模态的无破坏式扩展与知识保留，朝统一、可组合的多模态基础模型迈进一步；代码与检查点已开源（项目页提供）。

Abstract: Achieving true artificial general intelligence requires foundation models capable of integrating new modalities without forgetting prior knowledge. However, accommodating continuous generative objectives alongside discrete understanding tasks causes severe gradient conflicts. Existing architectures, including standard Mixture-of-Experts (MoE), are highly susceptible to representation overwriting. Even structurally partitioned paradigms like Mixture-of-Transformers (MoT) remain vulnerable to catastrophic forgetting, severely impeding multimodal scalability. In this work, we introduce Rosetta, a composable native multimodal pretraining framework designed for seamless and non-destructive modality expansion. Rosetta adopts a modular paradigm where core foundational knowledge is preserved within global shared experts, while modality-specific capabilities are distributed across plug-and-play experts. To guarantee non-destructive composition, we propose Momentum-Anchored Orthogonal Projection (MAOP). MAOP leverages the optimizer's momentum state as an implicit semantic anchor, selectively neutralizing conflicting gradient components from new modalities while preserving synergistic updates. Extensive evaluations demonstrate that, while standard MoE and MoT architectures suffer catastrophic forgetting of previously acquired knowledge, Rosetta robustly preserves established language and visual understanding. Furthermore, it delivers superior image generation and unlocks cross-modal synergy, paving the way for truly composable and unified multimodal foundation models. To facilitate further multimodal research, we release our code and checkpoints to the community. Project page at https://rosetta-lmm.github.io/.

</details>


### [25] [Learning When to Listen: Gated Affect Fusion for Human Motion Prediction](https://arxiv.org/abs/2607.00296)
*Jingni Huang*

Main category: cs.CV

TL;DR: 论文系统研究在真实无约束视频中，用面部情感特征辅助人体运动预测的价值与边界，提出带门控的跨模态Transformer以稳定融合；结论是情感只能在短中期提供有限增益，长期仍由运动学连续性主导。

  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 真实场景的人体运动预测存在未来行为多义性与多模态噪声；面部情感可能提供行为线索，但其实际效用、时域边界与在框架中的作用机制尚不清楚。

Method: 构建多模态管线：使用MediaPipe提取人体姿态轨迹，HSEmotion提取面部情感表示；提出Gated Affect Transformer（GAT），通过门控动态调节情感到姿态的跨模态信息流；采用严格的按受试者划分协议，进行多时间跨度评测，并设计置乱/随机情感的反事实实验检验门控作用。

Result: 简单的早期特征拼接比仅姿态基线更差；GAT 的门控可自适应抑制情感噪声并在可信情感信号下开启，从而稳定提升短中期预测；反事实实验显示门控能屏蔽无结构噪声；情感特征的有效预测窗口有限（约≤30帧），长期预测由运动学连续性主导。

Conclusion: 面部情感应被视为补充性而非主导性线索；选择性、门控式的多模态融合在现实场景更可靠；在短中期可适度利用情感，长期应依赖姿态与运动学建模。

Abstract: Human motion forecasting in unconstrained real-world videos remains challenging due to the ambiguity of future behaviors and the presence of noisy multimodal observations. While facial affect potentially provides complementary behavioral cues, its practical utility and mechanistic boundaries within motion forecasting frameworks remain poorly understood. In this work, we present a systematic study investigating the utility and temporal limitations of affect-conditioned forecasting in-the-wild. We establish a rigorous multimodal pipeline combining MediaPipe body pose trajectories with HSEmotion facial affect representations, and introduce the Gated Affect Transformer (GAT) to dynamically regulate cross-modal information flow. Through extensive multi-horizon evaluations under a strict subject-wise protocol, we demonstrate that naive early cross-modal concatenation consistently degrades forecasting accuracy relative to pose-only baselines. Conversely, our proposed gating mechanism stabilizes cross-modal integration by adaptively controlling the affective stream. Crucially, controlled counterfactual experiments using shuffled and randomized affect inputs reveal that the learned gate successfully suppresses unstructured cross-modal noise while remaining responsive to plausible affective signals. Furthermore, our empirical results indicate that facial affect features provide bounded, horizon-dependent predictive cues strictly within short-to-medium windows (e.g., 30 frames), whereas long-term trajectories remain predominantly governed by intrinsic kinematic continuity. Our findings provide empirical evidence that facial affect should be regarded as a complementary behavioral cue rather than a dominant driver of future motion, offering practical guidance for selective multimodal fusion in unconstrained human motion forecasting.

<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 小型多模态LLM参数预算有限，直接训练触觉模块会与现有视觉-语言推理争夺参数，导致灾难性遗忘或性能下降，需要一种既能学习新模态（触觉）又能保留原有视觉知识的方法。

Method: 1) 评估预训练参数的重要性，将参数空间划分为关键子空间（critical）与沉睡子空间（dormant）；2) 冻结关键子空间以作为稳定锚点保持通用视觉知识；3) 仅在掩码隔离的沉睡子空间上进行触觉-LLM对齐训练；4) 整体为选择性、非破坏性扩展，不增加LLM推理开销。

Abstract: Touch supplies the physical grounding needed to perceive intrinsic material properties, such as friction and compliance, that vision alone often cannot resolve. Recent efforts for equipping multimodal LLMs with this tactile sense, however, expose a zero-sum trade-off: the limited parameter budget of compact models forces a choice between acquiring the new sensory modality and preserving the established vision-language reasoning. We present Splash, a mask-isolated tactile alignment learning framework for MLLMs. Splash quantifies the significance of each pretrained parameter, and partitions the parameter space into a dormant and critical subspace. While the frozen critical subspace acts as a stable anchor to safeguard general visual knowledge, Splash updates the isolated dormant subspace to internalize tactile alignment towards LLMs. This selective, non-destructive expansion effectively prevents catastrophic forgetting and ensures non-destructive modality expansion. Extensive experiments show that Splash effectively achieves tactile reasoning without additional inference overhead in the LLM part, demonstrating state-of-the-art performance on visuo-tactile benchmarks, including SSVTP, TVL, and TacQuad, while preserving its original general-purpose capabilities.

### [27] [RetailSMV: Exocentric vs. Egocentric Adaptation of Foundation Video World Models in Retail](https://arxiv.org/abs/2607.00310)

<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 通用视频扩散模型在互联网上预训练，域外偏差明显，难以直接用于特定部署（如超市门店的店员操作）。在存在同步的第一人称（ego）与第三人称（exo）视频时，不清楚哪种视角更能高效地对世界模型进行域适配，从而提升零售任务中的生成与预测质量。

Method: 构建RetailSMV数据集：来自5家超市、以店员为主体、含同步ego/exo视角的32,105条带字幕片段（上货、摆放、称重、推补给车、收银扫描等）。在同一预训练基础模型Cosmos3-Nano上，用LoRA进行三种一致超参配置的适配：仅ego、仅exo、以及ego+exo组合。在200条留出测试集上，采用7种互补指标，并使用严格成对统计评估协议比较。

Result: 在6/7个点估计上，exo-only适配与组合适配相当或更优；在LPIPS、PSNR、DreamSim上显著优于组合，尽管exo-only仅使用15,985条exo片段（组合用32,105条）。对称成对比较显示：在ego-only训练中加入exo数据有帮助，而在exo-only训练中加入ego数据反而有害。适配带来的绝对提升在最短rollout时段最大，表明近地平线预测窗口最受益。

Conclusion: 对于零售场景，将通用视频扩散世界模型进行参数高效适配时，优先使用外部视角（exo）数据更有效；在资源受限下，exo-only优于或不逊于混合视角。域适配价值在短期预测最为突出，提示后续系统应优先优化近时域的生成与对齐。

Abstract: Foundation video diffusion models are increasingly viewed as world simulators for embodied agents, yet their pretraining on internet-scale generic video leaves them poorly aligned with real-world deployment domains. We study parameter-efficient adaptation of a pretrained foundation video world model to retail scenes: when synchronized egocentric and exocentric video of the same activity are available, which viewpoint of training data produces the strongest adapted model?
  We introduce RetailSMV (Retail Synchronized Multi-View), a corpus of 32,105 captioned retail clips from five supermarkets with synchronized ego/exo capture from the store-staff perspective (stocking, arranging, weighing, managing supply carts, scanning at checkout), rather than the customer-centric framing of prior retail video corpora, and train three matched Low-Rank Adaptation (LoRA) configurations of Cosmos3-Nano (egocentric-only, exocentric-only, combined) under identical hyperparameters. On a 200-clip held-out test set evaluated with seven complementary metrics under a strict paired statistical protocol, exocentric-only adaptation matches or exceeds combined adaptation on six of seven point estimates and is significantly better on LPIPS, PSNR, and DreamSim, despite training on only 15,985 exocentric clips (versus 32,105 for combined). A symmetric paired comparison further shows that adding exocentric data to egocentric-only training helps while adding egocentric data to exocentric-only training hurts. The absolute adaptation gap is largest at the shortest rollout time, identifying the near-horizon prediction window as the regime in which adaptation is most beneficial.

### [28] [Typography-Based Monocular Distance Estimation for Advanced Driver-Assistance Systems](https://arxiv.org/abs/2607.00319)
*Manognya Lokesh Reddy,Zheng Liu*

Main category: cs.CV

TL;DR: 用车牌字体尺度当作已知标准，单目相机即可精确估距，融合多种车牌排印特征与单幅深度网络，帧间平滑并输出距离/相对速度/TTC，达到<0.13 m误差，低成本补充雷达/激光/双目。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现有前向防碰、ACC、AEB常依赖雷达/激光/双目，成本与封装受限。作者观察到美国产车牌具有受法规约束的统一尺寸与字高，若能利用此“印刷标准尺”，则单目亦可恢复尺度与距离，降低成本并增强系统容错。

Method: 提出Typography-Based Monocular Distance Estimation：1) 车牌检测与发行州识别；2) 量测图像中字符高、笔画宽、字符间距与安装孔距等多种可观测量；3) 结合相机内参做投影几何换算，利用加权融合（对弱/受噪声量测赋予低权）并引入单幅深度网络作为辅证；4) 在时间维度上对距离、距离变化率与TTC进行平滑；5) 以美规预警时序触发碰撞预警。同时返回目标距离、方位与身份。

Result: 在不依赖测距硬件的条件下，基于单目与车牌排印特征实现距离估计，报告平均误差<0.13 m，并可稳定输出相对速度与TTC。

Conclusion: 车牌的标准化排印提供了可移植“尺度锚”，单目摄像头通过多特征与深度先验融合即可达到高精度、低成本、低维护的距离估计，作为雷达/激光/双目的容错与成本优化补充，且同时提供目标身份与方位信息。

Abstract: Estimating the distance to a leading vehicle is a basic input to forward collision warning, adaptive cruise control, and automated emergency braking. Production systems obtain this distance from radar, laser scanners, or stereo camera pairs, which add cost, power draw, and packaging constraints. This paper asks whether a single ordinary camera can recover the same distance by using a target that is standardized in size and present on every road vehicle: the rear license plate. U.S. plates share a fixed outer size and a character height that is set by regulation and varies only narrowly between states, so the height of a plate character in the image is a direct measure of distance once the camera geometry is known. The proposed method (Typography-Based Monocular Distance Estimation) detects the plate, measures the height of its printed characters, identifies the issuing state to select the correct physical character height, and recovers distance from the camera projection. Three measurements taken from the same plate: the character height, the stroke width, and the character spacing. Together with the spacing of the two mounting holes and a single-image depth network, are combined so that a weak or corrupted measurement is given less weight automatically. The distance, its rate of change, and a time-to-collision estimate are smoothed across frames and used to raise a warning with the timing used by U.S. collision-warning regulations. The same plate that anchors the scale also identifies the vehicle, so the method returns a distance, a bearing, and an identity from one passive sensor. It reads scale from a printed standard instead of from time of flight or parallax, making it a cheap, low-maintenance complement to those sensors in a fault-tolerant perception stack, achieving the cost-effective distance estimation with error less than 0.13 m.

### [29] [CORGI: Consistency-Aware 3D Dog Reconstruction from a Single Image in the Wild](https://arxiv.org/abs/2607.00321)
*Yuxiao Wu,Weile Li,Boyi Zhu,Yumeng Liu,Youcheng Cai,Ligang Liu*

<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 单张非受控图像重建高度关节化动物（如狗）的高质量3D极难：缺少多视角、生成不一致、难以细粒度几何和纹理恢复、以及无3D标注监督。

Method: 三组件流水线：1) CDOG：以“Canonical + Orbit”两类LoRA驱动，将任意输入姿态归一到规范姿态并合成360°环绕视频；2) CA-3DGS：在D-SMAL先验上构建一致性感知的可变形3D高斯，显式为每视角建模生成误差，通过神经形变场学习到精确的顶点位移；3) DCGR：自监督的形变条件生成修复，消除结构畸变、恢复高频细节。

Result: 在多数据集/多品种狗上实现SOTA：生成几何准确、视角一致、细节丰富且可动画的3D资产，适用于下游应用。

Abstract: Reconstructing high-fidelity 3D models of highly articulated animals, such as dogs, from a single in-the-wild image remains a formidable challenge. In this paper, we introduce CORGI, a novel framework for consistency-aware 3D dog reconstruction from a single unconstrained image that completely eliminates the need for 3D supervision. To overcome generative inconsistencies and the lack of multi-view capture, our pipeline introduces three core components. First, we propose a Canonical-Driven Orbital Generation (CDOG) strategy, utilizing specialized Canonical and Orbit LoRAs to normalize arbitrary input poses and synthesize reliable 360-degree video observations. Second, we design a Consistency-aware Deformable 3DGS (CA-3DGS) module that anchors on a D-SMAL prior, explicitly modeling per-view generative errors through dedicated neural deformation fields to learn accurate vertex-level displacements. Finally, to eliminate structural distortions and recover high-frequency details, we introduce a self-supervised Deformation-Conditioned Generative Repair (DCGR) module. Extensive experiments demonstrate that CORGI achieves state-of-the-art performance, generalizing seamlessly across diverse dog breeds to produce geometrically accurate, visually coherent, and fully animatable 3D assets ready for downstream applications.

### [30] [DroneFINE: Domain-Aware Parameter-Efficient Fine-Tuning of Vision-Language Detectors for Drone Images](https://arxiv.org/abs/2607.00338)
*Ke Wu,Yanan Zhang,Yingjie Gao,Wenhao Li,Chenyu Zhou,XinZhu Ma,Jiaxin Chen,Di Huang*

  <summary>Details</summary>

Method: 提出DroneFINE，由两部分组成：1) HyperAdapter：数据依赖、前景感知、多路径的适配机制，突破传统PEFT静态结构限制，实现动态与多通路调节以贴合航拍小目标与视角特性；2) SemanticGate：文本条件的背景抑制策略，引入“背景词表”引导模型主动压制无关区域响应，强化与文本提示的语义对齐。

Result: 在VisDrone与UAVDT上，DroneFINE较现有PEFT取得显著提升，并在仅需更少可训练参数的前提下，达到接近全量微调的检测性能。

While Vision-Language Models (VLMs) have offered a powerful solution for universal object detection, adapting them to UAV scenarios remains non-trivial due to a substantial domain gap between VLM pre-training data and aerial imagery. The prevailing Parameter-Efficient Fine-Tuning (PEFT) methods prove ineffective in bridging this gap, as VLMs' "natural-scene, foreground-dominant" visual priors misalign with the "bird's-eye-view, background-dominant, small-object" characteristics of UAV data. To address this issue, we propose DroneFINE, a novel PEFT paradigm comprising two domain-aware complementary modules tailored for VLM-based drone image detectors. Specifically, a data-dependent, foreground-aware, and multi-path adaptation mechanism named HyperAdapter is designed, which overcomes the static structural constraints of PEFT. In addition, a background suppression algorithm named SemanticGate is developed. It is a text-conditioned guidance strategy that employs background vocabulary to actively guide the model in suppressing responses from irrelevant regions. Extensive experiments on VisDrone and UAVDT demonstrate that DroneFINE significantly outperforms existing PEFT methods and achieves performance comparable to full fine-tuning while substantially reducing the number of trainable parameters.

### [31] [Personalized Object Identification and Localization via In-Context Inference with Vision-Language Models](https://arxiv.org/abs/2607.00357)
*Kensuke Nakamura,Byung-Woo Hong*

Main category: cs.CV

TL;DR: 提出POIL任务：在个性化少样本场景中，既要定位目标实例，又要拒绝不含该实例的查询图像；给出数据集与一种两步一体化的VLM方法IPLoc-ID，显著降低负样本误检且保持与IPLoc相当的定位性能。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现有POL方法（如IPLoc）默认查询图必含目标，现实中大量无关图像使该假设失效，导致高误检。需要能在少样本、实例级别下同时完成“是否存在”与“在哪里”的统一框架。

Method: 将问题扩展为POIL：在少样本检测框架中，给定带框参考图与标签，既进行实例级定位又执行存在性判别。提出IPLoc-ID：先用VLM进行候选框预测，再判断该框是否与参考实例匹配；通过自提问（self-posed query）把两步串联到同一自回归生成流程中；并构建公开来源的POIL数据集进行评测与消融。

Result: 在消融与全面实验中，IPLoc-ID在负样本（不含目标）上显著压制假阳性，同时在含目标图像上的定位精度与IPLoc相当。

Conclusion: IPLoc-ID有效解决更贴近实用的实例级POIL任务，弥补传统通用检测、少样本检测及仅定位的IPLoc在“存在性+定位”一体化上的不足。

Abstract: Personalized object localization (POL) localizes an object instance in a query image based on a few reference images with bounding-box annotations and a target object label. The pioneering method, IPLoc, solves this task through in-context inference with vision-language models (VLMs). However, it assumes that the query image always contains the target object. This assumption severely limits its applicability to real-world scenarios with many irrelevant images. To address this issue, we formulate a new task, personalized object identification and localization (POIL), by positioning POL within the broader few-shot object detection framework. POIL aims to localize the target object instance while rejecting query images that do not contain the reference object instance. We also present POIL datasets constructed from public sources. We further propose an in-context algorithm named IPLoc-ID for solving POIL with VLMs. IPLoc-ID first predicts a candidate bounding box and then determines whether it corresponds to the reference object instance. We introduce a self-posed query to connect these two steps within a single autoregressive generation framework. Through ablation studies and comprehensive experiments, we show that IPLoc-ID substantially suppresses false-positive detections on negative query images while maintaining localization performance comparable to IPLoc. Overall, IPLoc-ID effectively addresses the practical instance-level POIL task, which cannot be sufficiently solved by conventional object detection, few-shot object detection, or the localization-only IPLoc method.

</details>


### [32] [SFDATrack: Generalized Source-Free Domain Adaptive Tracking Under Adverse Weather Conditions](https://arxiv.org/abs/2607.00369)
*Siyuan Yao,Ziqi Wang,Ruiqi Yu,Junqi Huang,Wenqi Ren,Xiaochun Cao*

Main category: cs.CV

TL;DR: SFDATrack是一种源数据不可用场景下的目标跟踪方法，仅用目标域的不利天气样本即可自适应并实现稳健跟踪。其通过均值教师+DIM蒸馏出抗天气扰动的目标token，并用超球原型投影到多域原型上，联合约束域内特性与域不变性，从而在多种恶劣天气下取得领先性能。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现实部署常受隐私与存储限制，无法访问源域大规模视频；但现有自适应跟踪多依赖源+目标域数据，且恶劣天气（雨、雾、雪等）带来外观退化与分布偏移，导致鲁棒性下降。因此需要一种仅用目标域数据、仍能泛化到多种天气的源自由（source-free）自适应跟踪框架。

Method: 1) 采用mean-teacher骨干并引入Dual Interactive Mamba（DIM）块：对经数据增强的目标域样本进行一致性蒸馏，筛选/蒸馏出对天气变化更鲁棒的候选目标token。2) 提出超球原型投影（HPP）模块：将候选token投影到潜在超球空间中的多域原型上。通过对原型的域特异性与域不变性双重约束，学习既能区分不同天气域、又能共享跨域语义的表示，实现无源数据的自适应。3) 端到端适配并用于状态估计，提升跟踪鲁棒性与泛化性。

Result: 在多种基准上超过现有SOTA方法，表现出在雨、雾、雪等不利天气下的更强鲁棒性与泛化能力。

Conclusion: 源自由设定下，结合均值教师+DIM的鲁棒token蒸馏与超球多域原型投影，可在仅有目标域不利天气样本时实现有效域适配与强泛化，取得领先跟踪性能。

Abstract: Domain adaptive visual object tracking under adverse weather conditions has garnered significant attention in recent years. Despite the impressive performance, existing methods heavily rely on the large-scale video frames from both source and target domains, which is impractical under rigid resource constraints where source data is unavailable. To overcome this limitation, we propose SFDATrack, a generalized source-free domain adaptive tracker that merely leverages adverse weather samples from the target domain for robust state estimation. Specifically, SFDATrack first employs a mean-teacher backbone with Dual Interactive Mamba (DIM) blocks to distill the candidate target tokens that are resilient to weather variations from classified, augmented samples. Afterwards, we introduce a hyperspherical prototype projection (HPP) module to project these tokens onto multi-domain prototypes within a latent hyperspherical space. By enforcing both domain-specific and domain-invariant properties of the multi-domain prototypes, SFDATrack can be seamlessly adapted to diverse weather conditions with powerful generalizability. Extensive experiments evaluated on various benchmarks demonstrate that SFDATrack achieves superior performance compared to state-of-the-art approaches. The code is available at https://github.com/watcherBR0/sfdatrack.

### [33] [MEPA: Multi-Scale Representation Alignment for Visual Autoregressive Modeling with Mixture of Experts](https://arxiv.org/abs/2607.00371)
*Nuoyan Zhou,Zhijun Tu,Lei Yu,Kun Cheng,Jie Hu,Nannan Wang,Xinghao Chen*

Main category: cs.CV

TL;DR: 论文提出在视觉自回归(VAR)多尺度生成中引入“尺度感知、Token路由”的Mixture-of-Experts与残差特征聚合，以缓解跨尺度共享架构的冲突与早期尺度语义误差传播，显著提升训练效率与生成质量（ImageNet 256×256 上更低 FID、更少训练轮、更小参数）。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: VAR采用粗到细的多尺度自回归生成，但：1）低尺度负责全局语义，高尺度负责细节，共享同一架构导致优化目标冲突；2）自回归的因果性使早期尺度语义不准会层层放大，拖累最终质量。因此需要一种能按尺度解耦表示学习并强化早期语义的机制。

Method: 1）尺度感知Token路由MoE：为不同尺度引入可学习的门控/路由，使不同尺度选择不同专家，减少跨尺度耦合与冲突；2）外部自监督特征注入：在早期尺度引入外部预训练自监督特征；3）针对VAR设计的残差式特征聚合：非简单对齐，而是以残差融合方式将外部特征与自回归特征结合，稳健增强语义；4）保持总体训练开销几乎不变（路由成本小），同时降低总参数与训练轮数。

Result: 在ImageNet 256×256基准上，相比致密(dense)基线：更低的FID；仅需一半默认训练epoch即可达更好性能；参数规模更小；训练成本仅小幅增加；随着训练更久，性能优势进一步扩大。

Conclusion: 通过尺度感知MoE与残差式外部特征聚合，有效解耦多尺度表示学习并抑制早期语义误差传播，带来更快训练与更高图像质量；方法可作为通用模块集成到VAR类多尺度自回归生成框架中。

Abstract: Visual AutoRegressive modeling (VAR) has pioneered a coarse-to-fine multi-scale autoregressive generative paradigm, demonstrating strong capabilities in image generation. However, VAR still suffers from inherent deficiencies in multi-scale representation learning. Specifically, lower scales primarily capture global semantics, while higher scales focus on fine-grained details. Employing a shared architecture across scales induces optimization conflicts. Moreover, due to the causal autoregressive process, inaccurate semantics at early scales can propagate and significantly degrade the final output. To address these issues, we introduce a scale-aware token-routed Mixture of Experts (MoE) architecture, allowing scale-adaptive expert selection, thereby facilitating decoupled representation learning across scales. In addition, we enhance semantic modeling at early scales by incorporating external self-supervised features. Unlike naive alignment, we analyse and design a residual feature aggregation scheme tailored to the VAR paradigm. Extensive experiments show that our method significantly improves both training efficiency and generation quality. On the ImageNet 256*256 benchmark, our model achieves a superior FID compared to the dense baseline while requiring only half of the default training epochs and a smaller parameter budget, with a merely marginal increase in training cost. Moreover, the performance gap further widens with larger training epochs.

### [34] [Learning to Compose: Revisiting Proxy Task Design for Zero-Shot Composed Image Retrieval](https://arxiv.org/abs/2607.00374)
*Jingjing Zhang,Lei Zhang,Zheren Fu,Zhendong Mao*

Main category: cs.CV

TL;DR: 提出FoCo用于零样本合成图像检索，学习“关注→完成”的两阶段组合函数，通过文本锚定的视觉聚合与上下文条件的语义补全，配合跨实例对比训练，获得SOTA并具更强泛化。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现有ZS-CIR大多只强化图文表征并配合预设的固定组合方式（如向文本编码器注入伪词或线性特征算术），导致“组合函数”本身未被学习，难以表达多样且细粒度的语义修改。

Method: 将组合建模为两阶段：1) Focus：文本锚定的视觉聚合（依据局部化文本语义选择性汇聚参考图像中与修改相关的视觉内容）；2) Complete：上下文条件的语义补全（利用剩余场景上下文将聚合的视觉特征变换为一致的合成表示）。两任务联合训练，使用跨实例对比目标，鼓励语义多样、抑制捷径式组合策略。

Result: 在四个ZS-CIR基准上取得SOTA表现，并展现更好的跨数据集/分布的泛化能力。

Conclusion: 学习式两阶段组合函数能更准确地表达文本驱动的细粒度修改，优于依赖固定组合机制的ZS-CIR方法，具有更强鲁棒性与可迁移性。

Abstract: Composed Image Retrieval (CIR) retrieves a target image from a reference image and a textual modification. While supervised CIR relies on costly triplets, Zero-Shot CIR (ZS-CIR) alleviates this reliance through proxy tasks trained on image-text pairs. However, existing proxy tasks primarily enhance visual and textual representations to accommodate a predefined composition mechanism such as pseudo-word injection into a frozen text encoder or linear feature arithmetic. As a result, the composition function itself remains unlearned, limiting the model's ability to express diverse and fine-grained semantic modifications. To address this, we propose FoCo, which models composition as two coordinated stages: focusing on modification-relevant visual content, and then completing the target semantics. We realize these through two proxy tasks: text-anchored visual aggregation to selectively gather visual content guided by localized textual semantics, and context-conditioned semantic completion to transform these aggregated visuals with the remaining scene context into a coherent composed representation. The tasks are trained jointly with a cross-instance contrastive objective, encouraging semantic diversity and discouraging shortcut composition strategies. Extensive experiments on four ZS-CIR benchmarks show FoCo's state-of-the-art performance and improved generalization.

### [35] [LIST3R: Long-sequence Instance-aware 3D Reconstruction](https://arxiv.org/abs/2607.00375)
*Jing Gao,Wei Wang,Feiran Wang,Yan Yan*

Main category: cs.CV

TL;DR: 提出LIST3R：以“实例锚点”为核心的长序列3D重建框架，通过跨子序列匹配与对象约束，实现更一致的全局重建与更准确轨迹。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 长视频重建常因回访区域断裂、漂移与全局一致性差而失败。人类记忆会围绕稳定、可识别的对象组织空间信息，启发以“可跟踪实例”为锚点重连片段、减少累积误差。

Method: 将长视频划分为重叠子序列；对每个部分重建，构建含语义与几何证据的本地实例库并维护可持续跟踪的实例锚点；在子序列间匹配锚点以识别回访与重叠区域，并以对象感知的约束进行片段对齐；在全流程中用持续演化的几何证据更新本地库并逐步合并为全局实例库，最终形成一致的全局重建。

Result: 在长序列基准上，相较现有方法，获得更准确的相机轨迹与更高质量的3D重建，验证了实例锚点组织长时程重建的有效性。

Conclusion: 以实例锚点为核心的组织策略能稳健跨子序列连接与全局对齐，显著提升长序列3D重建的精度与一致性；代码已开源，便于复现与扩展。

Abstract: We present LIST3R, an instance-aware framework for long-sequence 3D reconstruction inspired by the way humans organize spatial memory around stable and recognizable objects. LIST3R organizes long-sequence reconstruction around instance anchors, using them to reconnect fragmented subsequences and consolidate local observations into a coherent global 3D scene. Given a long video, our approach partitions it into overlapping subsequences and builds a structured local instance library for each partial reconstruction, maintaining persistent trackable anchors with semantic and geometric evidence. These anchors are matched across subsequences to recover revisited regions and provide object-aware constraints for fragment alignment, producing a consistent global reconstruction. During this process, the evolving geometric evidence updates the local instance libraries and progressively organizes them into a unified global 3D instance library. Experiments on long-sequence benchmarks show that our method produces more accurate trajectories and higher-quality 3D reconstructions, highlighting the effectiveness of persistent instance anchors for organizing long-horizon 3D reconstruction. Our code is available on the project page: https://yixn965.github.io/LIST3R/.

</details>


### [36] [Radial Interaction Tomography: Recognizing Non-Transitive Evolutionary Games from One Range-Expansion Image](https://arxiv.org/abs/2607.00378)
*Faruk Alpay,Baris Basaran*

Main category: cs.CV

TL;DR: 该文提出从一次端点图像反演微生物扩张中各类型边界随半径演化的流场，并检验是否符合传递性的标量适应度层级。核心是将扇区边界在对数极坐标中提取为几何信号，证明可观测性与稳定性，并给出加权的传递/循环分解、完整接触的圆形实验设计、物理时钟与机制的不可辨识性、精确高斯循环性检验及多区间Bonferroni扫描。提供确定性基准与非学习仿真器，能从端点图像恢复配对边缘流史、在四类型扩张中检测循环残差，并用残差驱动无量纲的主动设计控制层，覆盖反应-扩散控制、表型前沿优化、协议合成、蒙特卡洛鲁棒性与群体状态衔接。

Conclusion: 端点图像蕴含足够几何信息以恢复多类型扩张的边界动力学，并可区分传递性标量适应度与循环交互。所提出的逆问题框架与统计检验既有理论可观测/稳定性保证，又给出实用实现与基准，为非学习、可解释的设计-控制闭环提供基础。

Abstract: Colored sectors in a microbial range expansion encode more than lineage survival counts. We formulate a computer-vision inverse problem: from one endpoint image of an accretive multi-type expansion, recover the radius-indexed pairwise boundary-flow field and test whether the visual pattern is compatible with a transitive scalar fitness hierarchy. The observable is a geometric signal extracted from sector-boundary curves in log-polar coordinates. We prove endpoint observability and stability for frozen fronts, weighted transitive/cyclic decomposition, contact-complete circular design, physical-clock and mechanism non-identifiability, exact Gaussian cyclicity testing, and Bonferroni-valid interval scanning. The benchmark is deterministic: analytic endpoint images, blurred/noisy pixel round trips, scalar-null stress tests, public-image tracing, multi-resolution mechanistic endpoints, and a non-learning frozen-front simulator. The implementation recovers pairwise edge-flow histories from endpoint images, detects cyclic residuals in a mechanistic four-type expansion, and uses those residuals as forcing signals for a dimensionless active design-control layer covering reaction-diffusion control, phenotype-frontier optimization, protocol synthesis, Monte Carlo robustness, and a downstream population-state bridge.

### [37] [Vitality-Aware Compression for Efficient Image-to-Shape Diffusion Transformers](https://arxiv.org/abs/2607.00382)
*Jaeah Lee,Hyunjin Kim,Jaewoong Cho,Gihyun Kwon*

Main category: cs.CV

TL;DR: 提出首个面向图像到3D形状的DiT压缩方法，在显著缩小模型体积的同时保持几何保真度；通过活性度引导的结构化剪枝、自适应量化与定向微调，实现最高66%模型尺寸压缩且生成质量接近原模型。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 3D形状生成虽有进展，但基于Diffusion Transformer的大模型在受限算力环境下难以部署；现有扩散模型压缩策略多针对图像/语音等域，难以直接迁移到3D；以往3D效率工作偏重推理加速而非主干压缩，亟需面向3D几何特性的专门压缩框架，以在不牺牲几何质量的前提下降低模型规模。

Method: 提出几何感知的压缩框架：观察到3D DiT各层对几何合成的重要性不均，定义“活性度/活力”(vitality)度量以排序层与模块；在此指导下执行（1）结构化剪枝：有选择地裁剪对几何不敏感的层/通道/注意力头；（2）自适应量化：对不同层按敏感度分配不同比特宽度；（3）定向微调：在保持关键几何层的同时对被压缩部分进行少量再训练以恢复性能。该流程作为插拔式框架适配多种image-to-3D DiT模型。

Result: 在多个SOTA图像到3D模型上实现最高66%的模型尺寸缩减；压缩后仍保持与全尺寸模型相当的几何/合成保真度；展示良好的通用性与可移植性。

Conclusion: 几何感知、活性度引导的组合压缩（剪枝+量化+微调）可在不显著牺牲质量的前提下大幅缩小image-to-shape DiT体积，为资源受限环境中的高保真3D生成提供可行的即插即用方案。

Abstract: We propose the first compression approach for image-to-shape Diffusion Transformers (DiTs) that substantially reduces model size while preserving geometric fidelity. Despite remarkable progress in 3D shape generation, large DiT-based models remain computationally prohibitive in resource-constrained settings. Furthermore, it is difficult to directly transfer existing diffusion model compression strategies developed for different domains to 3D generation, and prior 3D efficiency approaches focus primarily on inference speed rather than backbone compression. To address this limitation, we build a geometry-aware compression framework tailored to image-to-shape DiTs. Guided by the observation that 3D DiT layers exhibit non-uniform importance for geometry synthesis, we introduce a vitality-guided framework integrating structured pruning, adaptive quantization, and targeted fine-tuning. Our method achieves up to 66% model-size reduction across state-of-the-art image-to-3D models while maintaining synthesis fidelity comparable to full-sized counterparts. This highlights the potential of our framework as a plug-and-play solution for efficient 3D shape generation across diverse models.

### [39] [The Illusion of High Utility in Safety Alignment of Text-to-Image Diffusion Models](https://arxiv.org/abs/2607.00402)

Main category: cs.CV

TL;DR: 论文指出：现有T2I扩散模型的安全对齐在粗粒度指标下看似“又安全又有用”，但在细粒度语义忠实度评估（TIFA）上显著退化；作者发现原因在于文本编码器提示嵌入空间发生“语义塌缩”。为此提出SAGE结构感知几何正则化，在保持安全性的同时恢复结构化效用（TIFA较SOTA提升约+5%），且粗粒度指标仍具竞争力。
